			//window.requestAnimationFrame(function() {

					e.thumbhide = e.thumbhide===undefined ? 0 : parseInt(e.thumbhide);
					e.mh = e.mh===undefined || e.mh=="" || e.mh==="auto" ? 0 : parseInt(e.mh,0);

						newh = Math.max(e.mh,window.RSIH);					
					else{					
						e.gw = Array.isArray(e.gw) ? e.gw : [e.gw];
						for (var i in e.rl) if (e.gw[i]===undefined || e.gw[i]===0) e.gw[i] = e.gw[i-1];

							ix = 0,

</dom-module><dom-module id="paper-spinner-styles">
  <template>
    <style>
      /*
      /**************************/
      /* STYLES FOR THE SPINNER */
      /**************************/

      /*
       * Constants:
       *      ARCSIZE     = 270 degrees (amount of circle the arc takes up)
       *      ARCTIME     = 1333ms (time it takes to expand and contract arc)
       *      ARCSTARTROT = 216 degrees (how much the start location of the arc
       *                                should rotate each time, 216 gives us a
       *                                5 pointed star shape (it's 360/5 * 3).
       *                                For a 7 pointed star, we might do
       *                                360/7 * 3 = 154.286)
       *      SHRINK_TIME = 400ms
       */

      :host {
        display: inline-block;
        position: relative;
        width: 28px;
        height: 28px;

        /* 360 * ARCTIME / (ARCSTARTROT + (360-ARCSIZE)) */
        --paper-spinner-container-rotation-duration: 1568ms;

        /* ARCTIME */
        --paper-spinner-expand-contract-duration: 1333ms;

        /* 4 * ARCTIME */
        --paper-spinner-full-cycle-duration: 5332ms;

        /* SHRINK_TIME */
        --paper-spinner-cooldown-duration: 400ms;
      }

      #spinnerContainer {
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;

        /* The spinner does not have any contents that would have to be
         * flipped if the direction changes. Always use ltr so that the
         * style works out correctly in both cases. */
        direction: ltr;
      }

      #spinnerContainer.active {
        -webkit-animation: container-rotate var(--paper-spinner-container-rotation-duration) linear infinite;
        animation: container-rotate var(--paper-spinner-container-rotation-duration) linear infinite;
      }

      @-webkit-keyframes container-rotate {
        to { -webkit-transform: rotate(360deg) }
      }

      @keyframes container-rotate {
        to { transform: rotate(360deg) }
      }

      .spinner-layer {
        position: absolute;
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        opacity: 0;
        white-space: nowrap;
        color: var(--paper-spinner-color, var(--google-blue-500));
      }

      .layer-1 {
        color: var(--paper-spinner-layer-1-color, var(--google-blue-500));
      }

      .layer-2 {
        color: var(--paper-spinner-layer-2-color, var(--google-red-500));
      }

      .layer-3 {
        color: var(--paper-spinner-layer-3-color, var(--google-yellow-500));
      }

      .layer-4 {
        color: var(--paper-spinner-layer-4-color, var(--google-green-500));
      }

      /**
       * IMPORTANT NOTE ABOUT CSS ANIMATION PROPERTIES (keanulee):
       *
       * iOS Safari (tested on iOS 8.1) does not handle animation-delay very well - it doesn't
       * guarantee that the animation will start _exactly_ after that value. So we avoid using
       * animation-delay and instead set custom keyframes for each color (as layer-2undant as it
       * seems).
       */
      .active .spinner-layer {
        -webkit-animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate;
        -webkit-animation-duration: var(--paper-spinner-full-cycle-duration);
        -webkit-animation-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0.0, 0.2, 1);
        -webkit-animation-iteration-count: infinite;
        animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate;
        animation-duration: var(--paper-spinner-full-cycle-duration);
        animation-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0.0, 0.2, 1);
        animation-iteration-count: infinite;
        opacity: 1;
      }

      .active .spinner-layer.layer-1 {
        -webkit-animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-1-fade-in-out;
        animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-1-fade-in-out;
      }

      .active .spinner-layer.layer-2 {
        -webkit-animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-2-fade-in-out;
        animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-2-fade-in-out;
      }

      .active .spinner-layer.layer-3 {
        -webkit-animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-3-fade-in-out;
        animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-3-fade-in-out;
      }

      .active .spinner-layer.layer-4 {
        -webkit-animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-4-fade-in-out;
        animation-name: fill-unfill-rotate, layer-4-fade-in-out;
      }

      @-webkit-keyframes fill-unfill-rotate {
        12.5% { -webkit-transform: rotate(135deg) } /* 0.5 * ARCSIZE */
        25%   { -webkit-transform: rotate(270deg) } /* 1   * ARCSIZE */
        37.5% { -webkit-transform: rotate(405deg) } /* 1.5 * ARCSIZE */
        50%   { -webkit-transform: rotate(540deg) } /* 2   * ARCSIZE */
        62.5% { -webkit-transform: rotate(675deg) } /* 2.5 * ARCSIZE */
        75%   { -webkit-transform: rotate(810deg) } /* 3   * ARCSIZE */
        87.5% { -webkit-transform: rotate(945deg) } /* 3.5 * ARCSIZE */
        to    { -webkit-transform: rotate(1080deg) } /* 4   * ARCSIZE */
      }

      @keyframes fill-unfill-rotate {
        12.5% { transform: rotate(135deg) } /* 0.5 * ARCSIZE */
        25%   { transform: rotate(270deg) } /* 1   * ARCSIZE */
        37.5% { transform: rotate(405deg) } /* 1.5 * ARCSIZE */
        50%   { transform: rotate(540deg) } /* 2   * ARCSIZE */
        62.5% { transform: rotate(675deg) } /* 2.5 * ARCSIZE */
        75%   { transform: rotate(810deg) } /* 3   * ARCSIZE */
        87.5% { transform: rotate(945deg) } /* 3.5 * ARCSIZE */
        to    { transform: rotate(1080deg) } /* 4   * ARCSIZE */
      }

      @-webkit-keyframes layer-1-fade-in-out {
        0% { opacity: 1 }
        25% { opacity: 1 }
        26% { opacity: 0 }
        89% { opacity: 0 }
        90% { opacity: 1 }
        to { opacity: 1 }
      }

      @keyframes layer-1-fade-in-out {
        0% { opacity: 1 }
        25% { opacity: 1 }
        26% { opacity: 0 }
        89% { opacity: 0 }
        90% { opacity: 1 }
        to { opacity: 1 }
      }

      @-webkit-keyframes layer-2-fade-in-out {
        0% { opacity: 0 }
        15% { opacity: 0 }
        25% { opacity: 1 }

					<div class="entry-content">
					<div class="et-l et-l--post">
			<div class="et_builder_inner_content et_pb_gutters3"><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_5 et_pb_with_background et_section_regular et_had_animation" style="">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_5">

				<div class="et_pb_code_inner">
			<div id="catch-breadcrumb" class="catch-breadcrumb breadcrumb-area custom"><nav class="entry-breadcrumbs">

			<span class="breadcrumb"><a href="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/">Home</a><span class="sep">&gt;</span></span><span class="breadcrumb"><a href="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/childcare-programmes/">Programme</a><span class="sep">&gt;</span></span><span class="breadcrumb-current">Nursery 2 Montessori</span>
			</nav><!-- .entry-breadcrumbs --></div><!-- .breadcrumb-area -->

			<span id="bc_site"></span></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_6">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_6  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et_pb_column_empty">
				
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_7  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_5">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="95" height="79" src="https://brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2019/07/noun_Home_2344843.png" alt="home icon" title="home icon" class="wp-image-974"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_5  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h1 class="center" data-gtm-vis-recent-on-screen59696002_25="1213" data-gtm-vis-first-on-screen59696002_25="1213" data-gtm-vis-total-visible-time59696002_25="100" data-gtm-vis-has-fired59696002_25="1">Brighton Montessori: Nursery 2 Programme</h1></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_6  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><strong><u>4 years old</u></strong></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_8  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child et_pb_column_empty">
				
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_6 et_section_regular">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_7">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_9  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_7  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2><strong>Nurturing Curiosity and Cultivating Independence </strong></h2>
<p><strong></strong></p>
<p>Brighton Montessori is a quality kindergarten and nursery school with multiple centres conveniently located in Singapore. We provide personalized learning for all children under our care. The Nursery 2 curriculum is designed to provide a holistic and hands-on learning experience for young children. The curriculum focuses on the development of social skills, self-awareness, and independence which are essential to achieve success both academically and outside of school.</p>
<p>Our purposefully structured and immersive Montessori environment has intriguing materials within reach of children, motivating them to explore, interact and learn independently. At the N2 level, children will master the blending technique by the end of the year to prepare for early reading. They will also be able to understand and apply math concepts such as addition, subtraction and knowledge of teens and tens.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_10  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_6">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1000" height="801" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Image-1-N2-2.jpg" alt="" title="Image-1---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Image-1-N2-2.jpg 1000w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Image-1-N2-2-980x785.jpg 980w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Image-1-N2-2-480x384.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) and (max-width: 980px) 980px, (min-width: 981px) 1000px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3444"></span>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_7 et_section_regular">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_8">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_11  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_8  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2><strong>Why Should You Enroll Your Child into a Montessori Nursery 2 Programme in Singapore?</strong></h2>
<p><strong></strong></p>
<p>The Montessori approach highly values a child’s individuality and provides opportunities for children to acquire self-help skills that enable them to become independent learners. Each child is directed on their own path to maximize their potential. Our Montessori Nursery 2 Programme strikes a balance in both individual and group activities, that enable children to experience one-on-one teaching as well as group learning. </p>
<p>The weekly programme covers the five pillars of Montessori. We also provide holistic experiences with Music and Movement, Outdoor activities and Art and Craft throughout the week. Activities such as Current Issues, Environmental Issues, Brighton Talk and Show and Tell are introduced to equip children with public speaking skills. These opportunities help develop children’s communication and social skills in preschool.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_9">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_12  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_7">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="707" height="1000" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-1-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Collage-Image-1---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-1-N2.jpg 707w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-1-N2-480x679.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 707px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3447"></span>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_13  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_8">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="707" height="1000" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-2-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Collage-Image-2---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-2-N2.jpg 707w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-2-N2-480x679.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 707px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3448"></span>

				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="707" height="1000" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-3-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Collage-Image-3---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-3-N2.jpg 707w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Collage-Image-3-N2-480x679.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 707px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3449"></span>

				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1000" height="638" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Ratio-Image-N2-1.jpg" alt="" title="Ratio-Image---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Ratio-Image-N2-1.jpg 1000w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Ratio-Image-N2-1-980x625.jpg 980w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Ratio-Image-N2-1-480x306.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) and (max-width: 980px) 980px, (min-width: 981px) 1000px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3459"></span>

				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="865" height="300" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/1-10.png" alt="" title="1-10" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/1-10.png 865w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/1-10-480x166.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 865px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3453"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_9  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p style="text-align: center;"><em><span class="JsGRdQ">Teacher-to-Child Ratio</span></em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_12">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="751" height="297" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/icon1.png" alt="" title="icon1" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/icon1.png 751w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/icon1-480x190.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 751px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3455"></span>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_11">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_17  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_10  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2><strong>Personalized Attention &amp; Guidance</strong></h2>
<p><strong></strong></p>
<p>Our Nursery 2 classes have a teacher-to-child ratio of 1:10, which is lower than industry regulations in Singapore (1 + 1 para-educators/educarers: 20). Each teacher is trained in the Montessori method, and the centre is also supported by an Academic Coordinator. Children are naturally curious about everything at this age and require a higher level of attention. Therefore, a low teacher-to-child ratio allows our teachers to monitor your child’s development closely and allows them to connect with each child on a deep and personal level. Teachers can also better develop personalized goals and learning objectives for each N2 student.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_9 et_section_regular">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_12">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_18  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_11  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2><strong>Our Curriculum: The Montessori Approach</strong></h2>
<p><strong></strong></p>
<p>At Brighton Montessori, our Nursery 2 Programme covers the whole spectrum of Montessori training with the five pillars of Montessori. The five pillars are Practical Life Skills, Sensorial Exercises, Language, Mathematics, and Cultural Studies. Our educators encourage learning through hands-on activities in creative and fun ways. Our children are also exposed to other subjects to develop all-rounded abilities in preparation for formal schooling.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_13 et_pb_equal_columns">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_19  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_13">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="624" height="252" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon1.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon1.png 624w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon1-480x194.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 624px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3119"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_12  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Phonics</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_14">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Phonics-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Phonics---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Phonics-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Phonics-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3461"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_13  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Word-building exercises</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> using Large Moveable Alphabet to assimilate their knowledge of sounds in words.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">By the end of the Nursery 2 curriculum, children will be able to </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">read simple phrases, sentences, and short books</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">. Also, children will progress onwards from tracing to </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">writing short sentences</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> in this year.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Public speaking exercises conducted through the </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Brighton Talk</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> and</span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> Show and Tell</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> activities weekly. Opportunities to discuss</span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> current and environmental issues</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> are also integrated into the programme.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_20  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_15">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="347" height="341" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon2.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon2.png 347w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon2-300x295.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 347px) 100vw, 347px" class="wp-image-3126"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_14  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Math</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_16">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.jpg" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3128"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_15  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA align-start para-style-body direction-ltr"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Practice adding and subtracting under 10 using </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Short Bead Stair</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> and </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"><strong>Small Number Rods</strong>.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA align-start para-style-body direction-ltr"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">The</span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> Seguin Boards A and B</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> also introduce the concept of teens and tens to children using both </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">concrete and abstract materials</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA align-start para-style-body direction-ltr"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Children will be able to identify numbers up to </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">90</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_14 et_pb_equal_columns">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_21  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_17">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="330" height="338" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon3.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon3.png 330w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon3-293x300.png 293w" sizes="(max-width: 330px) 100vw, 330px" class="wp-image-3120"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_16  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Practical Life</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_18">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Practical-Life-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Practical-Life---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Practical-Life-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Practical-Life-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3467"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_17  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">At Nursery 2, our children </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">refine their motor skills</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> by working on more complex exercises such as use of scissors, threading and lock and keys.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Exercises such as use of paper clips, sharpener and ruler also equip them with the necessary skills to</span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> work independently</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> in the classroom.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_22  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_19">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="590" height="225" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon4.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon4.png 590w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon4-480x183.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 590px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3121"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_18  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Sensorial</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_20">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Sensorial-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Sensorial---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Sensorial-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Sensorial-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3468"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_19  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Integrate understanding</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> of math concepts via the use of sensorial materials.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Children are introduced to more </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">complex shapes</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> such as polygons, quadrilaterals and curve-sided shapes via the </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Geometric Cabinet</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">, explore relationships between various Geometric Solids and apply logic and creativity in assembling different designs using the Constructive Triangles.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_15 et_pb_equal_columns">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_23  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_21">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="672" height="227" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon5.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon5.png 672w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon5-480x162.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 672px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3122"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_20  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Cultural Studies</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_22">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Cultural-Studies-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Cultural-Studies---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Cultural-Studies-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Cultural-Studies-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3464"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_21  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Four Cultural Subjects</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> (History, Geography, Botany, Zoology) will be introduced throughout the year</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Subjects will be broken down into monthly interest topics such as </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Fruits and Vegetables for Botany</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">, </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Land </span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">and </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"><strong>Water Forms for Geography </strong></span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">etc. </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Specialized </span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Montessori </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">cultural materials</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> are used to help the children explore these ideas.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Festival Weeks</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> are also included to help children develop a </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">deep appreciation and understanding</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> of the </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">different cultures and traditio</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"><strong>ns</strong> that we have in Singapore.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_24  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_23">

			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_22  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Aesthetics &amp; Creativity</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_24">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Aesthetics-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Aesthetics---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Aesthetics-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Aesthetics-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3463"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_23  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Nursery 2 children are exposed to an array of art and music elements, to </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">apply their skills</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> and </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">develop appreciation </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">for these creative expressions.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Children will be introduced in a structured manner to different elements <strong>(</strong></span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Colour, Lines, Shape, Texture</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"><strong>)</strong> while using a variety of media and art tools. They can also share their reasoning behind the choices they make in the arts.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">In Music and Movement, the children’s </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">understanding of beat and rhythm</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> has been extended to include </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">tempo and dynamics</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> in Nursery 2.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_16 et_pb_equal_columns">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_25  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_25">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="387" height="328" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon7.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon7.png 387w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon7-300x254.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 387px) 100vw, 387px" class="wp-image-3124"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_24  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3><span class="S1PPyQ">Physical Activities</span></h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_26">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Physical-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Physical---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Physical-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Physical-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3466"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_25  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Physical movement is crucial for our young ones to develop healthy bodies and minds. We provide</span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> daily physical activities</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> both in </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">outdoor and indoor </span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">settings.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Playground facilities are available in all of our centres for our children.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">In Nursery 2, we focus more on coordination and control over various locomotor skills such as </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">running in a zig-zag manner</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">, </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">jumping over low obstacles</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> and using different sports equipments such as hockey sticks and bats to hit objects.</span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_26  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_27">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="541" height="229" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon8.png" alt="" title="" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon8.png 541w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/icon8-480x203.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 541px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3125"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_26  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3>Mandarin</h3></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_28">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="704" height="470" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Mandarin-N2.jpg" alt="" title="Mandarin---N2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Mandarin-N2.jpg 704w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Mandarin-N2-480x320.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 704px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3465"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_27  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Mandarin is conducted on a daily basis. Our Mandarin teachers are native speakers that </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">immerse </span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">the children in </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">the language and relevant contexts</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Children also progress onwards from </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">strokes to writing characters</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">, and learning how to use the vocabulary in different contexts.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Simple storybooks</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> are also used in the lessons to help children </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">bridge their understanding</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> of Mandarin.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body">
</p><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>

				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_28  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2 style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #ffffff;"><strong><span class="JsGRdQ">Benefits</span></strong><span class="JsGRdQ"> of our Montessori Nursery 2 Programme</span></span></h2></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_18">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_28  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_29">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="200" height="206" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/1.png" alt="" title="" class="wp-image-2805"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_29  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #ffffff;"><em><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Show </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">appreciation</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> and </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">understanding</span></strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> for the world around them</span></em></span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_29  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_30">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="200" height="206" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/2.png" alt="" title="" class="wp-image-2806"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_30  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #ffffff;"><em><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">Refine </span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"><strong>fine-motor</strong> skills</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none"> through completing more </span><strong><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">complex exercises</span></strong></em></span></p></div>
			</div>

<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-center para-style-body" style="text-align: center;"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">As your child progresses, they continue to develop a strong foundation and work on various skills, through the Montessori approach.</span></p></div>

				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_36">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="835" height="238" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/faq1.png" alt="" title="faq1" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/faq1.png 835w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/faq1-480x137.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 835px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3479"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_33  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">In Singapore, most children attend Nursery school at age 3, starting at Nursery 1 then progressing to Nursery 2 at 4 years old.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">The Nursery 2 curriculum at Brighton Montessori is extensively focused on building on foundational skills, refining them, and integrating them with other subjects and aspects outside of school. The children at Nursery 2 are also given opportunities to discuss and present during the weekly programme in front of their teachers and peers to develop and build on their communication skills.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_22">
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column et_pb_column_35  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_37">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="836" height="239" src="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/faq2.png" alt="" title="faq2" srcset="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/faq2.png 836w, https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/faq2-480x137.png 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) 836px, 100vw" class="wp-image-3480"></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_34  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p class="_04xlpA align-start para-style-body direction-ltr"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">At Brighton Montessori, we cover the five Montessori Subjects: Practical Life Skills, Sensorial Exercises, Language, Mathematics, and Culture Studies through an emphasis on learning through hands-on activities. Our centres are also purposefully structured to create an environment where our students are motivated to explore, interact and learn independently.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA align-start para-style-body direction-ltr"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">The Montessori approach focuses more on individualized learning for our students, which provides them with more freedom to learn at their own pace and cultivate their interests. Learn more about our approach </span><a href="https://www.brightonmontessori.com.sg/our-difference"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span class="WdYUQQ text-strikethrough-none text-decoration-underline">here</span></span></a><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">.</span></p>
<p class="_04xlpA direction-ltr align-start para-style-body"><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none">As toddlers are full of energy and curiosity, they require more attention and guidance to ensure they progress to meet their learning goals. At Brighton Montessori, our low teacher-child ratio in the Nursery 2 class of 1 teacher to 10 students allows our teachers to provide a higher level of attention to each student to facilitate their personal development and objectives.</span><span class="WdYUQQ text-decoration-none text-strikethrough-none white-space-prewrap"> </span></p></div>
			</div>
			</div>

        <script>
            jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
                var $flag = true;
                /* Blurbs as Tabs */
                $('.tab-title').each(function () {
                    var section_id = $(this).find("a").attr("data-class");

                    section_id = "." + section_id;
                    $(this).find("a").removeAttr("href");
                    if ($flag) {
                        $('.tab-title').removeClass("active-tab");
                        $(this).siblings().removeClass("active-tab");
                        //  $(this).addClass("active-tab");
                        $('.tab-content').hide();

                        // $(section_id).show();
                        $flag = false;
                    }

                    $(this).click(function () {
                        if ($(this).hasClass("active-tab")) {
                            console.log('hide');
                            $('.tab-title').removeClass("active-tab");
                            $(section_id).hide();
                        } else {
                            console.log('shoe');
                            $('.tab-title').removeClass("active-tab");
                            $(this).siblings().removeClass("active-tab");
                            $('.tab-content').hide();
                            $(this).addClass("active-tab");
                            $(section_id).show();
                        }

                    });
                });
            });
        </script>

      :host > ::slotted(button) {
        position: relative;
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        margin: 0;
        padding: 0;
        background: none;
        border: none;
        outline: none;
        vertical-align: middle;
        color: inherit;
        cursor: pointer;
        /* NOTE: Both values are needed, since some phones require the value to be `transparent`. */
        -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);
        -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;
      }
      :host > ::slotted(button[disabled]) {
        color: #9b9b9b;
        pointer-events: none;
        cursor: auto;
      }
    </style>
    <slot></slot>
  </template>
</dom-module>

<dom-module id="paper-icon-button">
  <template strip-whitespace="">
    <style>
      :host {
        display: inline-block;
        position: relative;
        padding: 8px;
        outline: none;
        -webkit-user-select: none;
        -moz-user-select: none;
        -ms-user-select: none;
        user-select: none;
        cursor: pointer;
        z-index: 0;
        line-height: 1;

        width: 40px;
        height: 40px;

        /* NOTE: Both values are needed, since some phones require the value to be `transparent`. */
        -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);
        -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;

        /* Because of polymer/2558, this style has lower specificity than * */
        box-sizing: border-box !important;

        @apply --paper-icon-button;
      }

      :host #ink {
        color: var(--paper-icon-button-ink-color, var(--primary-text-color));
        opacity: 0.6;
      }

      :host([disabled]) {
        color: var(--paper-icon-button-disabled-text, var(--disabled-text-color));
        pointer-events: none;
        cursor: auto;

        @apply --paper-icon-button-disabled;
      }

      :host([hidden]) {
        display: none !important;
      }

      :host(:hover) {
        @apply --paper-icon-button-hover;
      }

      iron-icon {
        --iron-icon-width: 100%;
        --iron-icon-height: 100%;
      }
    </style>

    <iron-icon id="icon" src="[[src]]" icon="[[icon]]" alt$="[[alt]]"></iron-icon>
